< pics>
[{'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipOveaPyJhkkpxZ1h48QMDi3tNbO0S5wd4_iMqwP=w150-h150-k-no-p']}]<//pics>
< Text>
Great park! This one is closer to me so I have spent a lot of time here as a child so it has a real nostalgic value to it. Not going to lie though, this park is not nearly as pretty as the other parks around Moorpark. It doesn't have the view of Mammoth Park, nor the playground equipment like Miller has now. But gosh dang it is a wholesome place to be!

I love the layout of the place and it is pretty dog-friendly as well since the grass is pretty far removed from the playground area.
